



(declare-sort Unit)
(declare-datatypes (T1 T2) ((Pair (mk-pair (left T1) (right T2)))))
(define-fun gte ((x Int) (y Int)) Int (if (>= x y) 1 0))
(define-fun lte ((x Int) (y Int)) Int (if (<= x y) 1 0))
(define-fun eq ((x Int) (y Int)) Int (if (= x y) 1 0))
